 barsaat ke do maheene in subjiyon ke bharose hi vanavaasi apane parivaar ko jinda rakhte hai

 Earlier, the forest dwellers considered their rights and rights over the forest wealth, and by collecting gum, honey, gooseberry, pickle, leopard and sitaphal in the cities and towns, they used to eradicate the hunger of their family, but now the forest department has its right over the forest estate

 What is digital currency? Digital currency is a virtual currency operating on the Internet
 internet par is virtual karency kii shuruyaat janvari 2009 main bitcoin ke naam se hui thi

 District Judge IS Mehta ordered Liaqat to be released on bail on a personal bond of Rs 20,000 and bail of the same amount
 adaalat ne liyakat ko jamaanat pradaan karte hue kai sharten lagaayi hai or unhen adaalat kii purvanumati ke bina desh chhodkar nahin jane kaa nirdesh diya he
 Liaquat, 45, was arrested along with his family on March 20 while crossing the indo-nepal border in Gorakhpur, Uttar Pradesh
 liyakat kaa kahana tha ki vah jammu-kashmir sarkaar kii punarvaas niti ke tahat aatmasamarpan karne ke liye aayaa tha
 The comments seemaa paar karne ke turant baad use giraftaar karne vaali dilli police ne aarope lagaaya tha ki liyakat rashtriya rajdhani main holi se purv aatankwaadi hamale karne kii sajeesh main shaamil tha
 On March 28, the Ministry of Home Affairs issued a notification to the NIA after contradictory statements from Delhi and Jammu and Kashmir Police about Liaqat's arrest
 jila nyaayadhish aies mehta ne 20 hajaar rupee ke nijee muchalke tathaa itani hi raashi kii jamaanat dene par liyakat ko jamaanat par reeha karne ke aadesh die
 The court has imposed several conditions granting bail to Liaquat and directed him not to leave the country without the prior approval of the court
 45varshiya liyakat ko unke parivaar ke saath 20 march ko uttar pradesh ke gorakhpur main bharat-nepal seemaa paar karte samay giraftaar kiya gaya tha
 Liaquat said that he had come to surrender under the rehabilitation policy of the Jammu and Kashmir government
 tippaniyan The Delhi Police, who arrested him soon after crossing the border, alleged that Liaquat was involved in a conspiracy to carry out terror attacks in the national capital before Holi

 dilli ke indira gandhi stadium main desh ke tamaam bade udyogpatiyon ke bich pradhanmantri ne daawa kiya ki ye ek daur kii shuruyaat he, ek nae bharat ke aagaaz kaa elaan he

 com / qrmm0aykjo@therahulmahajan@atheist_krishna radhe maa theme kitty party The Nidahas T20 Trophy starts in Sri Lanka from today
 yuvaaon se saji b team bhejne ke baavjood bharat is trikoniya siries kaa prabal daavedaar mana ja rahaa he
 You must know why India sent a second-class team for this tournament, but it would not be known why this series is being played or why this tournament has been named Nidahas Trophy
 isliye aaie jaanate hai kyon yah siries srilanka team ke liye khaas he or bharat ko prabal daavedaar kahe jane ke baad bhi srilanka is trophy ko har haal main jeetna chahega
 The Nidahas Trophy is a triangular T20 series
 isamen bharat or srilanka ke alaava teesri team bangladesh he
 The tournament is being organized to mark 70 years of Sri Lankan independence
 yahi vajah he ki is toornament ko nidahas tii-20 trophy kaa naam diya gaya he
 Nidahas / Nidhas is the Sinhalese language of Sri Lanka, which means independence

 aresas ne nai ganavesh dhaaran karne ke liye vijaydashami kaa din is liye chunaa he ki aresas kii sthapana vijaydashami ke din 1925 main hui thi

 ab tak 3 baar kiya ganavesh main badlaav1925 main jab sangh kii sthapana ke samay khaaki kameez, khaaki nekar, chamade kii belt, kaale juute or kaali topi ko hi ganavesh main shaamil kiya gaya tha
 There have been 3 changes in the uniform of the Sangh before and with Mohan Bhagwat being the Sangh head, this is going to be the second change in the uniform
 ganavesh main badlaav k saath-sathsanshapani image bhi badalane kii koshish karegaa
 The first change that took place during Hedgewar: The Sangh first made changes to its uniform in 1939, when the Sangh chief was Hedgewar, who founded the union
 tab sangh ne khaaki kameez ko badalakar safed kameez kiya tha
 The Sangh then believed that their uniform was very similar to the dress of the British Army, keeping this in mind, this first change was made
 juuton or belt main bhi kiya gaya badlaavsangh ne apni veshbhusha main doosraa badlaav san 1973 main kiya gaya tha, us vakt sangh pramukh bala sahab devaras the
 Weightless shoes were then used in army uniforms, as in military uniforms
 tab swayamsevak ne vajandaar juuton kii jagah normal kaale juute rakhe the
 And the third change in uniform was done in 2010 itself
 is baar chamade kii belt kii jagah kapade kii belt ko ganavesh main shaamil kiya gaya tha

 us samay pratinidhi sabha ne is prastaav ko ye kehete hue taal diya tha kii is par ek vistrut report taiyaar kii jaaegi, jiske liye 5 saal kaa samay tay kiya tha

 bisisiai ne iske jawaab main kaha tha ki vah is kathith emoyu ko maanane ke liye baadhya nahin he or yah koi myne nahin rakhata, kyonki pakistan ne bharat dwaara sujhaaye isisi ke rajasav model par samarthan kii patibaddhta puri nahin kii
 The ICC then set up a three-member dispute redressal committee to consider the pcb's compensation claim
 is maamle kii sunwaayee ek se teen oktober tak yahaan isisi ke mukhyalay main hui
 Former Foreign Minister Salman Khurshid was among those who were cross-examined during the hearing
 bisisiai ke varisht adhikari ke anusaar khurshid ne suraksha kaarnon se pakistan ke saath dwipaksheeya cricket khilne se inkaar karne ke bharat ke rukh ko uchit tehraaya tha
 a condom manufacturer has dragged the Center to the Delhi High Court, suspecting that it may be denied a contract contract of more than 10 crore condoms, despite beating the rest in the tender process
 is maamle main nijee company ne sarkaar ke pichley saal ke us faisle kaa hawala diya, jisamen usne nijee company kii ‘safal boli’ ko nazarandaaj karte hue ek saarvajanik kshetra nigam (piesu) kocondomki aapurti main shaamil karne kaa faisla kiya tha
 The High Court in its interim order directed the Center not to cancel the tender process for the supply of male contraceptives to be distributed by recognized social health workers under the National Rural Health Mission
 usne kaha ki antarim aadesh nivida ke aade nahin aayega
 The court was hearing a petition filed by a private company called MHL Healthcare Limited
 is yachika main company ne shankaa jaahir kii thi ki pichley saal kii tarah centre is baar bhi puri prakriya radd kar saktaa he
 a bench of Justices Badar Duraj Ahmed and Justice Sanjeev Sachdeva said, 'this petition has been filed by the petitioner on the basis of the suspicion that every time the tender is withdrawn, it will give the L1 (lowest price offer ) And then the tender is rejected
 is baar bhi nivida ke khaarij kar die jane ke sanshay ke saath vah court ke samaksh aayaa he
 No order for cancellation of tender should be passed by the next date of hearing in this case
 'court neswasthya or parivaar kalyaan mantralayase bhi kaha ki vah do saptaah ke bheetar is yachika par apana ek javaabi halafanama de
 With this, the court adjourned the hearing of the case to 14 July
 peeth ne us echelel lifecare limited (bharat sarkaar kaa upkram) ko notice jari kiya, jise pichley saal nivida radd hone ke baad condom aapurti kaa order swasthya or parivaar kalyaan mantralay ne diya tha
 Senior Advocate D
 while favoring MHL in court
 krishnan ne kaha ki pichhali baar bhi sarkaar ne aapurti kii nivida ek sarkari agency ko nijee company dwaara prastaavit keemat kii tulana main kahin 'oonche daam' par de di thi
 MHL said that last time too she was the 'top bidder' for the supply of contraceptives
 mantralay ne nivida radd kar di thi or order echelel lifecare limited ko de diya gaya tha
 180 for 100 pieces per order to HLL Lifecare Limited
 77 rou kii keemat par 20 karod condom kii aapurti ke liye diya gaya tha
 The bench said that it would hear the case on merits of the case after all the defendants filed a counter affidavit on this petition
 pichley saal saat november ko centre ne court ko bataaya tha ki usne purush garbh nirodhakon kii aapurti kii nivida radd kar di he or nai prakriya shuru kii ja chuki he
 Is Gundaraj still running in Uttar Pradesh? Is it a crime in UP to expose the handiwork of someone through RTI? 29-year-old Anoop Singh of Dankour might have felt the same
 thekedaar ke khilaaf aawaaj uthaane or shikaayat karne kii evaj main anup ko agava kar liya gaya or chaar dinon tak bandhak banaakar unhen buree tarah torchar kiya gaya
 The miscreants lit them with cigarettes, fired them with an iron rod and hit them badly
 unke sharir par koi aisi jagah nahin, jahaan jakhm na hon
 Anoop is hospitalized in Greater Noida in a badly injured condition
 haalanki ab police ne maamla darj kar chaanbin shuru kar di he
 Actually Anup Singh is a BJP worker and his wife Pinki is a member of BDC i
e
 Regional Panchayat in Dankour
 bataaya gaya he ki anup singh artiai ke sahare jaankaree jutaney main lage rahete the or unhone kuch vakt purv ek thekedaar ke khilaaf shikaayat bhi kii thi
 Anoop of Sakka village complained to Yamuna Expressway Authority and after that investigation was also conducted
 isi dauraan, anup ko dhamkiyaan aane lageen or unhone iske liye police se madad bhi maangi
 On the morning of 13 December, Anoop left Dankour on his bike, then he was abducted by four people on the way
 iske baad unhen bulandshahr ke ek makaan main le jaaya gaya
 Here the miscreants gave them nothing to eat nor drink for four days
 badmaashon ne unhen buree tarah torchar kiya
 The body was smoked with cigarettes and also burnt with hot iron bars
 anup unase raham kii bheekh maangate rahe, lekin badmaash nahin maane
 Finally, four days later, the miscreant escaped by throwing him at a petrol pump in Bulandshahr area
 kisi tarah logon ne unke bare main jaankaree jutai or anup ko greater noida ke aspataal main bhartee karaayaa gaya
 He has more than 50 bruises all over his body
 is maamle kii soochna milane ke baad dancor kotwali main apharan or marpet kaa maamla darj kar liya gaya
 According to Anoop's uncle Charan Singh, he had been receiving threats from the contractor for a long time, as Anoop had complained to him about not working properly in the streets of the village
 anup kii patni pinki kaa kahana he ki anup ke saath aisa bartaav karne waalon ko kadi se kadi sajaa milani chahie
 Massive leaks of more than 10 million tax documents have exposed the secret bargaining of several stars, including Russian President Vladimir Putin's allies, global leaders and Barcelona player Lionel Messi
 isamen 500 se adhik bharatiyon kaa naam bhi he
 These documents have been investigated by more than 100 media groups and termed it as one of the biggest such investigations in history
 is jaanch main lagbhag 140 raajnneetik hastiyon kii sampatti se judi gupt saudebaaji ko ujagar kiya gaya
 These political personalities include 12 current or former heads of state
 itani badi sankhya main ye record german akhbaar sudushe jitung ne ek agyaat sutara se praapt kiye hai or ise antarrashtriya khoji patrkaar sangh (isiaije) ke jariye duniya bhar ke media ke saath saajha kar diya

 pradhanmantri pad ke bhaajapa ummidavaar narendra modi ne pradhanmantri manmohan singh ke purv media salaahkaar sanjay baru dwaara likhi gai kitaab kii ore ishaara karte hue 'sonia gandhi ke pradhanmantri karyaalay se pehle sarkari filein dekhne' ke aarope par congress adhyaksh se jawaab maanga
 Modi pointed to Baru's memoir 'the Accidental Prime Minister', which caused a stir in political circles, one of the biggest revelations in a book
 isamen daawa kiya gaya ki sonia pradhanmantri karyaalay (piemo) se pehle filon kaa nipataara karti thim
 She used to decide on government appointments, posts of ministries, transfers etc
 and then the Prime Minister mechanically approved it without any mind
 modi party ummidavaar anil shirole ke samarthan main shanivaar raat ek chunavi raily ko sambodhit kar rahe the
 He said, the dignity of the post of Prime Minister was reduced
 kitaab main kiye gaye khulaason ke 24 ghante baad bhi sonia ne chuppi sadhi hui he
 They should answer the allegations, because people want to know
 narendra modi ne kaha, hamane remote control ke bare main suna tha, lekin is maamle main remote khud hi sarkaar chalaa rahaa he
 He said that if the dignity of the Prime Minister is reduced in the same way, then no country in the world will accept its constitutional right
 modi ne kaha, kitaab main kiye gaye khulaason main shahjade (rahul gandhi) ke asanyamit karrwai ko bhi spasht kiya he, jinhone kaha tha ki mantrimandal or pradhanmantri dwaara manjuur kiye gaye (nirvaachit pratinidhiyon kii sajaa par) adhyadesh ko faad dena chahie
 These serious allegations have been made in a book written by an insider
 saansthanik apmaan ke udhaaharan dete hue bhaajapa netaa ne kaha, rashtriya salaahkaar parishad (enesi) ke gathan ke saath yojana ayog (adhyaksh) ke rup main pradhanmantri ke adhikaar ko bhi kamatar kiya gaya, jisane faisla lete samay unhen andhere main rakhaa
 irctc's target of raising 645 crores from IPO may be on the stock market on October 14 Everyone is waiting for the IPO of Listing Indian Railway Catering and Tourism Corporation (IRCTC)
 intjaar kii yah ghadi khatm hone vaali he
 Actually, the estimated deadline for the allotment of the initial public offering of IPC ie IRCTC is Thursday i
e
 today
 aise main is baat kii ummid kii ja rahi he ki share bazaar ke band hone se pehle iarsitisi ke ipo kaa alotment ho jayega
 What does this mean? Allotment means that the fate of those who have applied for participation in the IPO of IRCTC will be decided today
